
## What changed

### Frontend
- `sentence_inspector.tsx` `SourceCard`: when `source.full_text_available === false`, render `inspector-paywalled-{idx}` badge alongside tier badge. Source URL + tier + trace + snippet-fallback span all preserved.
- `verified_report_view.tsx` `SentenceRow`: now accepts `pool` prop and computes `t1_conflict` heuristic — set of distinct T1-source ids cited. ≥2 → render `inspector-t1-conflict` caption with explicit "may conflict — review Inspector" framing (honest substrate per CLAUDE.md §9.4).
- `verified_report_view.tsx` `SectionCard`: threads `pool` to `SentenceRow`. `VerifiedReportView` threads `pool` to `SectionCard`.

### Demo fixture
- New `SRC_PAYWALLED` source (T1, full_text_available=false, snippet only).
- POOL `sources_per_tier.T1` updated 12 → 13 per Codex iter-1 P2.
- sec_x:23 cites paywalled source.
- sec_x:24 cites src-0 with two spans, second out-of-range (5000-5050 vs ~80-char text).
- sec_x:25 cites BOTH src-0 AND src-1 (both T1) for T1-conflict heuristic.

### Playwright spec
- 4 tests: paywalled badge + URL still actionable; out-of-range second span flagged; T1-conflict on row; T1-conflict NOT on single-T1 sentence (negative test).

- `npx tsc --noEmit` (web/): exit 0.

  99: function SpanQuote({
 100:   token,
 101:   text,
 102:   idx,
 103:   spanIdx,
 104: }: {
 105:   token: ParsedToken;
 106:   text: string;
 107:   idx: number;
 108:   spanIdx: number;
 109: }) {
 110:   const out_of_range = token.end > text.length;
 111:   const span = out_of_range ? "" : text.slice(token.start, token.end);
 112:   if (out_of_range) {
 113:     return (
 114:       <p
 115:         data-testid={`inspector-span-out-of-range-${idx}-${spanIdx}`}
 116:         className="text-rose-700 dark:text-rose-300"
 117:       >
 118:         (span out of range: {token.start}-{token.end} of {text.length})
 119:       </p>
 120:     );
 121:   }
 122:   return (
 123:     <blockquote
 124:       data-testid={`inspector-span-${idx}-${spanIdx}`}
 125:       className="border-l-2 border-yellow-400 bg-yellow-50 px-2 py-1 italic dark:bg-yellow-900/20"
 126:     >
 127:       {span || "(empty span)"}
 128:     </blockquote>
 129:   );
 130: }

  76: function SentenceRow({
  77:   sentence,
  78:   show_dropped,
  79:   sentence_id,
  80:   hovered_id,
  81:   onSelect,
  82:   pool,
  83: }: {
  84:   sentence: ReportVerifiedSentence;
  85:   show_dropped: boolean;
  86:   sentence_id: string;
  87:   hovered_id: string | null;
  88:   onSelect: (id: string, sentence: ReportVerifiedSentence) => void;
  89:   pool: EvidencePool | null;
  90: }) {
  91:   const dropped = !sentence.verifier_pass;
  92:   if (dropped && !show_dropped) return null;
  93: 
  94:   // I-f5-010: T1-conflict HEURISTIC — when ≥2 distinct T1 sources are cited
  95:   // for one sentence, surface a "may conflict — review Inspector" caption.
  96:   // Honest framing per CLAUDE.md §9.4: this is NOT a semantic conflict
  97:   // detector; it's a flag prompting human review.
  98:   const t1_conflict = (() => {
  99:     if (!pool || dropped) return false;
 100:     const cited_t1 = new Set<string>();
 101:     for (const tok of sentence.provenance_tokens) {
 102:       const m = tok.match(/^\[#ev:([a-zA-Z0-9_\-]+):/);
 103:       if (!m) continue;
 104:       const src = pool.sources.find((s) => s.source_id === m[1]);
 105:       if (src && src.tier === "T1") cited_t1.add(m[1]);
 106:     }
 107:     return cited_t1.size >= 2;
 108:   })();
 109: 
 110:   return (
 111:     <li
 112:       data-testid={dropped ? "dropped-sentence" : "kept-sentence"}
 113:       data-sentence-id={sentence_id}
 114:       role="button"
 115:       tabIndex={0}
 116:       onClick={() => onSelect(sentence_id, sentence)}
 117:       onKeyDown={(e) => {
 118:         if (e.key === "Enter" || e.key === " ") {
 119:           e.preventDefault();
 120:           onSelect(sentence_id, sentence);
 121:         }
 122:       }}
 123:       className={cn(
 124:         "flex cursor-pointer flex-col gap-1 rounded-md border px-3 py-2 text-sm transition-colors focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-400 focus:outline-none",
 125:         dropped
 126:           ? "text-muted-foreground border-rose-500/30 bg-rose-500/5 line-through"
 127:           : "border-border bg-background",
 128:         hovered_id === sentence_id && "bg-yellow-100 dark:bg-yellow-900/40",
 129:       )}
 130:     >
 131:       <div className="flex items-start gap-2">
 132:         {(() => {
 133:           const surface = sentence.assertion_surface ?? "prose";
 134:           if (surface === "prose") return null;
 135:           return (
 136:             <span
 137:               data-testid={`surface-badge-${surface}`}
 138:               title={`Assertion surface: ${SURFACE_LABEL[surface]} (gated through Inspector)`}
 139:               className="inline-flex shrink-0 items-center rounded-full border border-blue-500/40 bg-blue-500/10 px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium tracking-widest text-blue-700 uppercase dark:text-blue-300"
 140:             >
 141:               {SURFACE_LABEL[surface]}
 142:             </span>
 143:           );
 144:         })()}
 145:         <span className={cn(dropped ? "" : "text-foreground")}>
 146:           {sentence.sentence_text}
 147:         </span>
 148:       </div>
 149:       {sentence.provenance_tokens.length > 0 && !dropped ? (
 150:         <span className="text-muted-foreground font-mono text-[10px]">
 151:           {sentence.provenance_tokens.join(" ")}
 152:         </span>
 153:       ) : null}
 154:       {dropped && sentence.drop_reason ? (
 155:         <span className="text-[10px] tracking-widest text-rose-700 uppercase dark:text-rose-300">
 156:           dropped — {DROP_REASON_LABEL[sentence.drop_reason as DropReason]}
 157:         </span>
 158:       ) : null}
 159:       {t1_conflict ? (
 160:         <span
 161:           data-testid="inspector-t1-conflict"
 162:           title="Multiple T1 sources cited — they may conflict; review Inspector. Heuristic flag, not a semantic conflict detection."

 164:         >
 165:           ⚠ T1 sources may conflict — review Inspector
 166:         </span>

 168:     </li>

 172: function SectionCard({
 173:   section,
 174:   show_dropped,
 175:   hovered_id,
 176:   onSelect,
 177:   pool,
 178: }: {
 179:   section: VerifiedReportSection;
 180:   show_dropped: boolean;

+  })();

 204:       </div>
 205:       <p
 206:         data-testid={`inspector-trace-${idx}`}
 207:         className="text-muted-foreground"
 208:       >
 209:         <strong className="text-foreground">{source.title}</strong>
 210:         {source.publication_date && <> · {source.publication_date}</>}
 211:         {source.authors[0] && (
 212:           <>
 213:             {" "}
 214:             · {source.authors.slice(0, 2).join(", ")}
 215:             {source.authors.length > 2 ? " et al." : ""}
 216:           </>
 217:         )}
 218:       </p>
 219:       <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
 220:         {tokens.map((tok, j) => (
 221:           <SpanQuote
 222:             key={j}
 223:             token={tok}
 224:             text={text}
 225:             idx={idx}
 226:             spanIdx={j}
 227:           />
 228:         ))}
 229:       </div>
 230:     </div>
 231:   );
 232: }
 233: 
 234: export function SentenceInspector({
 235:   open,
 236:   onOpenChange,
 237:   sentence,
 238:   sentence_id,
 239:   pool,
 240: }: {
 241:   open: boolean;
 242:   onOpenChange: (next: boolean) => void;
 243:   sentence: ReportVerifiedSentence | null;
 244:   sentence_id: string | null;
 245:   pool: EvidencePool | null;
 246: }) {
 247:   const tokens = sentence ? parseAllTokens(sentence.provenance_tokens) : [];
 248:   const pool_index = new Map(pool?.sources.map((s) => [s.source_id, s]) ?? []);
 249:   const grouped: Map<string, ParsedToken[]> = new Map();
 250:   for (const tok of tokens) {
 251:     const arr = grouped.get(tok.source_id) ?? [];
 252:     arr.push(tok);
 253:     grouped.set(tok.source_id, arr);
 254:   }
 255:   const groups = [...grouped.entries()];
 256:   return (
 257:     <Sheet open={open} onOpenChange={onOpenChange}>
 258:       <SheetContent
 259:         data-testid="sentence-inspector-sheet"
 260:         side="right"
 261:         className="data-[side=right]:w-full data-[side=right]:sm:w-2/5 data-[side=right]:sm:max-w-none"
 262:       >
 263:         <SheetHeader>
 264:           <SheetTitle data-testid="sentence-inspector-id">
 265:             {sentence_id ?? "Sentence inspector"}
 266:           </SheetTitle>
 267:           <SheetDescription>
 268:             Provenance and verification details for the selected sentence.
 269:           </SheetDescription>
 270:         </SheetHeader>
 271:         <div className="flex flex-col gap-3 px-4 pb-4 text-sm">
 272:           {sentence && (
 273:             <>
 274:               <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2">
 275:                 <p
 276:                   data-testid="sentence-inspector-text"
 277:                   className="text-foreground flex-1"
 278:                 >
 279:                   {sentence.sentence_text}
 280:                 </p>
 281:                 <div className="flex flex-col items-end gap-1">
 282:                   <AgreementBadge
 283:                     evaluator_agrees={sentence.evaluator_agrees}
 284:                   />
 285:                   {sentence.is_synthesis_claim ? <SynthesisClaimBadge /> : null}
 286:                 </div>
 287:               </div>
 288:               {tokens.length === 0 ? (
 289:                 <p className="text-muted-foreground text-xs italic">
 290:                   No provenance tokens.
 291:                 </p>
 292:               ) : (
 293:                 <div
 294:                   data-testid="inspector-sources"
 295:                   className="flex flex-col gap-2"
 296:                 >
 297:                   {groups.map(([source_id, group_tokens], i) => (
 298:                     <SourceCard
 299:                       key={source_id}
 300:                       tokens={group_tokens}
 301:                       source={pool_index.get(source_id)}
 302:                       idx={i}
 303:                     />
 304:                   ))}
 305:                 </div>
 306:               )}
 307:               {sentence.drop_reason && (
 308:                 <p
 309:                   data-testid="sentence-inspector-drop"
 310:                   className="text-xs tracking-widest text-rose-700 uppercase dark:text-rose-300"
 311:                 >
 312:                   dropped —{" "}
 313:                   {DROP_REASON_LABEL[sentence.drop_reason as DropReason]}
 314:                 </p>
 315:               )}
 316:             </>
 317:           )}
 318:         </div>
 319:       </SheetContent>
 320:     </Sheet>
 321:   );
 322: }

 458: // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 459: // Slice 002 — Clinical Retrieval (verified clinical sources)
 460: // Mirrors src/polaris_graph/retrieval2/evidence_pool.py +
 461: // api/retrieval_route.py.
 462: // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 463: 
 464: export type RetrievalSourceTier = "T1" | "T2" | "T3";
 465: 
 466: export interface RetrievalSource {
 467:   source_id: string;
 468:   url: string;
 469:   domain: string;
 470:   tier: RetrievalSourceTier;
 471:   title: string;
 472:   publication_date: string | null;
 473:   authors: string[];
 474:   snippet: string;
 475:   full_text_available: boolean;
 476:   full_text: string | null;
 477:   fetched_at_utc: string;
 478:   provenance: Record<string, unknown>;
 479:   retracted?: boolean;
 480: }
 481: 
 482: export interface RetrievalAdequacyVerdict {
 483:   is_adequate: boolean;
 484:   sources_per_tier: Record<RetrievalSourceTier, number>;
 485:   min_required_per_tier: Record<RetrievalSourceTier, number>;
 486:   failure_reason: string | null;
 487: }
 488: 
 489: export interface EvidencePool {
 490:   pool_id: string;
 491:   decision_id: string;
 492:   sources: RetrievalSource[];
 493:   adequacy: RetrievalAdequacyVerdict;
 494:   queries_executed: string[];
 495:   retrieval_started_at_utc: string;
 496:   retrieval_finished_at_utc: string;
 497:   latency_ms: number;
 498:   cost_usd: number;
 499: }
 500: 
 501: export interface RetrievalSuccessResponse {
 502:   error: false;
 503:   pool: EvidencePool;
 504:   server_time_utc: string;
 505: }
 506: 
 507: export interface RetrievalErrorBody {
 508:   error: true;
 509:   code: "wrong_status" | "wrong_scope_class" | "fetch_backend_unavailable";
 510:   message: string;
 511:   decision_id: string | null;
 512: }
 513: 
 514: export class RetrievalBadRequestError extends Error {
 515:   code: RetrievalErrorBody["code"];
 516:   decision_id: string | null;
 517:   constructor(body: RetrievalErrorBody) {
 518:     super(body.message);
 519:     this.name = "RetrievalBadRequestError";
 520:     this.code = body.code;
 521:     this.decision_id = body.decision_id;
 522:   }
 523: }
 524: 
 525: export async function runRetrieval(
 526:   decision: IntakeScopeDecision,
 527: ): Promise<RetrievalSuccessResponse> {
 528:   const response = await fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/api/retrieval`, {
 529:     method: "POST",
 530:     headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
 531:     body: JSON.stringify({ decision }),
 532:   });
 533: 
 534:   if (response.status === 400) {
 535:     const detail = await response.json().catch(() => null);
 536:     const body = (detail?.detail ?? detail) as RetrievalErrorBody | null;
 537:     if (body && body.error) {
 538:       throw new RetrievalBadRequestError(body);
 539:     }
 540:   }
 541: 
 542:   return asJsonOrThrow<RetrievalSuccessResponse>(response);
 543: }
 544: 
 545: export interface RetrievalHealthResponse {
 546:   status: "ok";
 547:   slice: string;
 548:   pipeline_stages: string[];
 549:   fetch_backend: string;
 550: }
 551: 
 552: export async function getRetrievalHealth(): Promise<RetrievalHealthResponse> {
 553:   const response = await fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/api/retrieval/health`);
 554:   return asJsonOrThrow<RetrievalHealthResponse>(response);
 555: }
 556: 
 557: /** Convenience: count sources matching a given tier. */
 558: export function countSourcesByTier(
 559:   pool: EvidencePool,
 560:   tier: RetrievalSourceTier,
 561: ): number {
 562:   return pool.sources.filter((s) => s.tier === tier).length;
 563: }
 564: 
 565: /** Convenience: dedupe + sort sources by tier (T1 first), then by domain. */
 566: export function sortSourcesByTier(
 567:   sources: RetrievalSource[],
 568: ): RetrievalSource[] {
 569:   const tier_rank: Record<RetrievalSourceTier, number> = {
 570:     T1: 0,
 571:     T2: 1,
 572:     T3: 2,
 573:   };
 574:   return [...sources].sort((a, b) => {
 575:     const t = tier_rank[a.tier] - tier_rank[b.tier];
 576:     if (t !== 0) return t;
 577:     return a.domain.localeCompare(b.domain);
 578:   });
 579: }

   1: // I-f5-003 — frontend mirror of polaris_graph.generator2.provenance.
   2: 
   3: const TOKEN_RE = /^\[#ev:([a-zA-Z0-9_\-]+):(\d+)-(\d+)\]$/;
   4: 
   5: export interface ParsedToken {
   6:   raw: string;
   7:   source_id: string;
   8:   start: number;
   9:   end: number;
  10: }
  11: 
  12: export function parseProvenanceToken(token: string): ParsedToken | null {
  13:   const match = TOKEN_RE.exec(token.trim());
  14:   if (!match) return null;
  15:   return {
  16:     raw: token,
  17:     source_id: match[1],
  18:     start: parseInt(match[2], 10),
  19:     end: parseInt(match[3], 10),
  20:   };
  21: }
  22: 
  23: export function parseAllTokens(tokens: string[]): ParsedToken[] {
  24:   return tokens
  25:     .map(parseProvenanceToken)
  26:     .filter((t): t is ParsedToken => t !== null);
  27: }
